<script>
    // Use custom variables from typoscripth
    var isStartpage = 0;
    var reloadDuration = 30;

    // Settings according to COPE
    const siteId = '54198';
    const networkId = '1003';
    const setupDomain = 'https://styria.smartadserver.com';

    // Other constants
    const websiteWidth = 1024;
    const websiteMarginLeft = 60;
    const windowWidth = $(window).width();

    // Configuration of formatIds
    var formatIds = {
        superbanner: {
            title: 'superbanner',
            show: false,
            formatId: '22374',
            name: 'SuperBanner-FullBanner1 (728x90)'
        },
        billboard: {
            show: false,
            formatId: '23170',
            name: 'Billboard (970x250 px oder 950x250 px)'
        },
        medrec1: {
            show: false,
            formatId: '22373',
            name: 'MedRec1 (300x250 px)'
        },
        medrec2: {
            show: false,
            formatId: '23175',
            name: 'MedRec2 (300x250 px)'
        },
        sitebar: {
            show: false,
            formatId: '22375',
            name: 'Sitebar/HPA/Sky (300x600 px, 160x600 px)'
        },
        bannerweb1: {
            show: false,
            formatId: '23362',
            name: 'mma-banner1-web – 300x250px, 300x600px'
        },
        bannerweb2: {
            show: false,
            formatId: '23366',
            name: 'mma-banner2-web – 300x250px, 300x600px'
        }
    };
    initFormatIds();

    // Variables
    var pageName = ((isStartpage) ? 'home' : 'ros');
    var target = ((isStartpage) ? 'homepage=true' : '');
    var formats = getFormatIdsToLoad();

    // Start with sas configuration
    var _sasConfig = {
        networkid : networkId,
        timeOut : 1000,
        enableLogging : false,
        placement : {
            siteId : siteId,
            pageName : pageName,
            formats: formats,
            target : target
        },
        partners : {
            '1plusX' : {
                'enabled' : true
            }
        }
    };

    // Setup
    var sas = sas || {};
    sas.cmd = sas.cmd || [];
    sas.cmd.push( function () {
        sas.setup({
            networkid : networkId,
            domain : setupDomain , //Smart BaseURL
            async : true ,
            renderMode : 2
        });
    });

    /**
     * Method initialies the formatIds array.
     * It checks the currently given conditions and therefore, sets
     * the appropriate formatId to 'show' is true.
     */
    function initFormatIds() {
        // Billboard+Superbanner OR Superbanner OR none (none is default)
        var billboardMinWidth = 992; // Responsive breakpoint
        var superbannerMinWidth = 728; // Width of superbanner
        if (windowWidth - billboardMinWidth >= 0) {
            formatIds.billboard.show = true;
            formatIds.superbanner.show = true;
        } else if (windowWidth - superbannerMinWidth >= 0) {
            formatIds.superbanner.show = true;
        }

        // Sitebar: It at least needs 300px right of the website to show
        var sitebarMinWidth = 300 + websiteWidth + websiteMarginLeft;
        if (windowWidth - sitebarMinWidth >= 0) {
            formatIds.sitebar.show = true;
        }

        // medrec1+2 OR bannerweb1+2
        var medrecMinWidth = 500;
        if (windowWidth - medrecMinWidth >= 0) {
            formatIds.medrec1.show = true;
            formatIds.medrec2.show = true;
        } else {
            formatIds.bannerweb1.show = true;
            formatIds.bannerweb2.show = true;
        }
    }

    /**
     * According to the formatIds object, return the to be loaded
     * formatIds.
     */
    function getFormatIdsToLoad() {
        var ids = [];
        for (formatId in formatIds) {
            if (`${formatIds[formatId].show}`.toLowerCase() === "true") {
                ids.push({ id: `${formatIds[formatId].formatId}`});
            }
        }
        return ids;
    }
</script>

<div class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0 frame-space-after-20" id="c3543">
<h2>Günstig tanken in Österreich </h2>
<p>Die Preistransparenzdatenbank liefert</p>
<ul>
<li>für Diesel/Super 95</li>
<li>für jedes Bundesland</li>
<li>auf einen Maus-Klick<br/>  </li>
</ul>
<p>die 5 günstigsten Tankstellen pro Bezirk.</p>
</div>

<div class="center-ad" id="sas_22373"></div>

                "S98": "0",
                "S95": "1.374",
                "N": "0",
                "D": "1.368",
                "G": "0",
                "zip": "1230",
                "land": "at",
                "bundesland": "Wien",
                "city2": "Liesing",
                "city": "Wien",
                "strasse": "Wien Breitenfurter Strasse 261 (Hofer-Parkplatz)",
                "date": "9.11.2021",
                "time": "1:41:33"
            }
        },
        {
            "type": "Feature",
            "geometry": {
                "type": "Point",
                "coordinates": [
                    11.420114,
                    47.278697
                ]
            },
            "properties": {
                "id": "INFT-C8FE5J",
                "name": "Diskont Tankstelle",
                "S98": "0",
                "S95": "1.524",
                "N": "0",
                "D": "1.489",
                "G": "0",
                "zip": "6020",
                "land": "at",
                "bundesland": "Tirol",
                "city2": "Innsbruck",
                "city": "Innsbruck",
                "strasse": "Hallerstraße 93 (Hofer Parkplatz)",
                "date": "9.11.2021",
                "time": "1:41:17"
            }
        }
    ]
}
,
      stations: [],
      datatable: null,
      getBundesland: "",
      getKraftstoff: "",
      initialSearchTerm: '', // Suchbegriff
      initialSortCol: 4, // Kraftstoff: s

      // Prepare the variables
      prepareVariables: function() {

        // Get url params for "bundesland" and "kraftstoff" and set the search and sorting field accordingly
        var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        if (urlParams.has("bundesland")) {
          arboe.getBundesland = urlParams.get("bundesland");
          arboe.initialSearchTerm = arboe.getBundesland;
        }
        if (urlParams.has("kraftstoff")) {
          arboe.getKraftstoff = urlParams.get("kraftstoff");
          if (arboe.getKraftstoff == "s") {
            arboe.initialSortCol = 4;
          } else if (arboe.getKraftstoff = "d") {
            arboe.initialSortCol = 5;
          }
        }
      },

      // Prepare the station data
      prepareStations: function() {

        arboe.json.features.forEach(function (item, index) {
          var s = (item.properties.S95 == 0 ? 'unbekannt' : item.properties.S95);
          var d = (item.properties.D == 0 ? 'unbekannt' : item.properties.D);
          var station = new Array(
            item.properties.name,
            item.properties.bundesland,
            item.properties.zip,
            item.properties.city,
            s,
            d,
            "<a href='https://map.arboe.at/tankstellen?gas_station=" + item.properties.id + "' target='_blank' title='Link zur ARBÖ Karte'><img src='/typo3conf/ext/arboe_contents/Resources/Public/Icons/maps.png' style='width:25px;' /></a>",
          );
          // Skip following gas stations:
          // - Empty name
          // - Both prices empty
          if (item.properties.name != '' || (item.properties.s == '' && item.properties.d == '')) {
            arboe.stations.push(station);
          }
        });
        arboe.populateDataTable();
      },
      populateDataTable: function() {
        arboe.datatable = $("#stations").DataTable({
          mark: true,
          'sDom': '<"H"<"colviz">lTfr><"clear">t<"F"ip>', // Need to add a clear div for Chris Firefox Browser!
          'data': arboe.stations,
          'aaSorting': [[ arboe.initialSortCol, "asc"]], // Which shown column, starting with 0
          'search': {
            'search': arboe.initialSearchTerm
          },
          'iDisplayLength': 25,
          'oLanguage': {
            'sLengthMenu': 'Anzeigen von _MENU_ Tankstellen',
            'sSearch' : '',
            'sZeroRecords' : '',
            'oPaginate': {
              'sFirst': '',
              'sLast': '',
              'sNext': '',
              'sPrevious': '',
            },
            'sInfo': 'Anzeige von Tankstellen _START_ bis _END_ (insgesamt _TOTAL_)',
            'sInfoFiltered': '',
          },
          'columns': [
            { width: "30%" }, // Name
            { width: "15%" }, // Bundesland
            { width: "8"}, // PLZ
            { width: "21"}, // Ort
            { width: "15%" }, // Super 95
            { width: "6%" }, // Diesel
            { width: "5%", "className":"text-center" }, // Link zu Karte
          ],
          "initComplete": function() {
            console.log("init complete");
          }
        });
      },
    };

    // On document load, prepare the variables, and populate the datatable
    $(function() {
      arboe.prepareVariables();
      arboe.prepareStations();
    });
  </script>
<table class="table table-striped tablesorter" id="stations">
<thead class="thead-light">
<tr>
<th scope="col">Name</th>
<th scope="col">Bundesland</th>
<th scope="col">PLZ</th>
<th scope="col">Ort</th>
<th scope="col">Super 95</th>
<th scope="col">Diesel</th>
<th scope="col"></th>

<div class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0 frame-space-after-20" id="c6066">
<p>Die angezeigten Treibstoffpreise entstammen der Preistransparenz-Datenbank. Das Preistransparenzgesetz, BGBl. I Nr. 54/2011, sowie die Preistransparenzverordnung, BGBl. II Nr. 246/2011, verpflichtet alle Tankstellenbetreiber in Österreich, Preisänderungen bei Superbenzin 95 und Dieselkraftstoff zu melden und jeweils umgehend in die Preistransparenz-Datenbank einzutragen. Die Energie-Control Austria ist durch das Gesetz mit dem Betrieb der Preistransparenz-Datenbank betraut. Für die Richtigkeit, Vollständigkeit und Aktualität der von den Tankstellenbetreibern eingegebenen Angaben kann keine Haftung übernommen werden.</p>
